I gave up trying to clean up the grammar file alone.
Ravi HELP ME...

There are lots of things wrong with the .jay file, but MonoBASIC is 
'makeable', and even accepts some .vb files as input.

Miguel, I´ve created a GenericParser class and now my .jay file has 
MoboBASICParser inherit from it, the only other change I had to make was in 
the modifiers.cs file that was referencing CSharpParser, now it invokes 
GenericParser.error(). If you like the idea I can change my makefile to use 
../mcs/*.cs and use your sources directly, if you dislike it I´ll keep just 
replicating the files.

I disrupted some parsing ability I had yesterday, because I have to change 
the basic tokens list, to reflect changes between beta 1 and beta 2. MS has 
changed mind about many issues in the vb side (in contrast c# is nearly 
unchanged).

Rafael Teixeira
Brazilian Developer
